â”‚  Agent: Crew Manager                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Task: IMPORTANT: If file output/system-design.md in the output directory exists, skip instruction in below. Do not create system design again. Take the requirements    â”‚
â”‚  described here and analyze/prepare a system design for coworkers. You identify requried modules to achieve the requriements. Each module should includes classes and    â”‚
â”‚  functions, describing the functionality.                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  Requirements:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  A simple account management system for a trading simulation platform.                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  The system should allow users to create an account, deposit funds, and withdraw funds.                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  The system should allow users to record that they have bought or sold shares, providing a quantity.                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  The system should calculate the total value of the user's portfolio, and the profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                   â”‚
â”‚  The system should be able to report the holdings of the user at any point in time.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  The system should be able to report the profit or loss of the user at any point in time.                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  The system should be able to list the transactions that the user has made over time.                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  The system should prevent the user from withdrawing funds that would leave them with a negative balance, or                                                             â”‚
â”‚   from buying more shares than they can afford, or selling shares that they don't have.                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚   The system has access to a function get_share_price(symbol) which returns the current price of a share, and includes a test implementation that returns fixed prices   â”‚
â”‚  for AAPL, TSLA, GOOGL.                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Do not develop python code by yourself.                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  1. Check if 'output/system-design.md' exists. If it does, skip this task. 2. If the file does not exist, gather the requirements for the account management system      â”‚
â”‚  from the task description. 3. Identify the necessary modules required to fulfill the requirements. Modules will include: UserAccount, Transaction, Portfolio, and       â”‚
â”‚  Market. 4. In the UserAccount module, define classes and functions for creating accounts, depositing, and withdrawing funds. 5. In the Transaction module, define       â”‚
â”‚  classes and functions for recording buy/sell transactions and ensuring that users cannot buy shares without sufficient funds or sell shares they do not own. 6. In the  â”‚
â”‚  Portfolio module, define methods to calculate the total value, report holdings, and assess profit/loss. 7. Integrate the 'get_share_price(symbol)' function, citing     â”‚
â”‚  where it would be used, specifically during transactions. 8. Compile all this information into a markdown document structured clearly with headings, modules            â”‚
â”‚  specified, and functionality described. 9. Utilize the File Writer Tool to save this document as 'system-design.md' in the './output' directory.                        â”‚

â”‚  # Account Management System Design for Trading Simulation Platform                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Introduction                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  This document outlines the design for a simple account management system for a trading simulation platform. The system supports account creation, deposits and          â”‚
â”‚  withdrawals of funds, transaction recording for buying and selling shares, and reporting of portfolio values and profit/loss.                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Required Modules                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  1. **UserAccount**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Responsible for managing user accounts, including fund deposits and withdrawals.                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  2. **Transaction**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Manages the recording of transactions and enforces trading rules such as sufficient funds and share ownership.                                                       â”‚
â”‚  3. **Portfolio**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     Handles the reporting of holdings, total value calculation, and profit/loss assessments.                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  4. **Market**                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚     Integrates with market functions, including fetching current share prices.                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Module Details                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  ### 1. UserAccount Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `UserAccount`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `user_id`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      - `balance`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `create_account(user_id)` - Creates a new user account.                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      - `deposit(amount)` - Increases the balance of the user account.                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      - `withdraw(amount)` - Decreases the balance; ensures it does not go negative.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2. Transaction Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Transaction`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `transactions`                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `buy_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the purchase of shares, checks if sufficient funds are present.                                                          â”‚
â”‚      - `sell_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the sale of shares, checks if the user owns a sufficient quantity.                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3. Portfolio Module                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Portfolio`                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `holdings`                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `calculate_total_value()` - Totals the current value of all shares based on market prices.                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `report_holdings()` - Lists current holdings and their quantities.                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚      - `assess_profit_loss()` - Calculates and reports profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4. Market Module                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  #### Functions:                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - `get_share_price(symbol)`                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    - **Description:** Fetches the current price of a share based on the symbol provided. This function is critical during transactions for checking share prices.        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Conclusion                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  This design outlines the necessary modules with their respective functionalities to achieve user account management in a trading platform simulation. Each module       â”‚
â”‚  focuses on specific areas ensuring clarity and separation of concerns.                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Next Steps                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  Implement the modules as specified, ensuring proper testing and validation of functionality to create a robust trading simulation experience.                           â”‚

â”‚  # Account Management System Design for Trading Simulation Platform                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Introduction                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  This document outlines the design for a simple account management system for a trading simulation platform. The system supports account creation, deposits and          â”‚
â”‚  withdrawals of funds, transaction recording for buying and selling shares, and reporting of portfolio values and profit/loss.                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Required Modules                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  1. **UserAccount**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Responsible for managing user accounts, including fund deposits and withdrawals.                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  2. **Transaction**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Manages the recording of transactions and enforces trading rules such as sufficient funds and share ownership.                                                       â”‚
â”‚  3. **Portfolio**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     Handles the reporting of holdings, total value calculation, and profit/loss assessments.                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  4. **Market**                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚     Integrates with market functions, including fetching current share prices.                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Module Details                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  ### 1. UserAccount Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `UserAccount`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `user_id`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      - `balance`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `create_account(user_id)` - Creates a new user account.                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      - `deposit(amount)` - Increases the balance of the user account.                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      - `withdraw(amount)` - Decreases the balance; ensures it does not go negative.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2. Transaction Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Transaction`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `transactions`                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `buy_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the purchase of shares, checks if sufficient funds are present.                                                          â”‚
â”‚      - `sell_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the sale of shares, checks if the user owns a sufficient quantity.                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3. Portfolio Module                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Portfolio`                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `holdings`                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `calculate_total_value()` - Totals the current value of all shares based on market prices.                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `report_holdings()` - Lists current holdings and their quantities.                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚      - `assess_profit_loss()` - Calculates and reports profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4. Market Module                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  #### Functi...                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚  # Account Management System Design for Trading Simulation Platform                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Introduction                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  This document outlines the design for a simple account management system for a trading simulation platform. The system supports account creation, deposits and          â”‚
â”‚  withdrawals of funds, transaction recording for buying and selling shares, and reporting of portfolio values and profit/loss.                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Required Modules                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  1. **UserAccount**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Responsible for managing user accounts, including fund deposits and withdrawals.                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  2. **Transaction**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Manages the recording of transactions and enforces trading rules such as sufficient funds and share ownership.                                                       â”‚
â”‚  3. **Portfolio**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     Handles the reporting of holdings, total value calculation, and profit/loss assessments.                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  4. **Market**                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚     Integrates with market functions, including fetching current share prices.                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Module Details                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  ### 1. UserAccount Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `UserAccount`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `user_id`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      - `balance`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `create_account(user_id)` - Creates a new user account.                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      - `deposit(amount)` - Increases the balance of the user account.                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      - `withdraw(amount)` - Decreases the balance; ensures it does not go negative.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2. Transaction Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Transaction`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `transactions`                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `buy_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the purchase of shares, checks if sufficient funds are present.                                                          â”‚
â”‚      - `sell_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the sale of shares, checks if the user owns a sufficient quantity.                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3. Portfolio Module                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Portfolio`                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `holdings`                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `calculate_total_value()` - Totals the current value of all shares based on market prices.                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `report_holdings()` - Lists current holdings and their quantities.                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚      - `assess_profit_loss()` - Calculates and reports profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4. Market Module                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  #### Functions:                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - `get_share_price(symbol)`                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    - **Description:** Fetches the current price of a share based on the symbol provided. This function is critical during transactions for checking share prices.        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Conclusion                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  This design outlines the necessary modules with their respective functionalities to achieve user account management in a trading platform simulation. Each module       â”‚
â”‚  focuses on specific areas ensuring clarity and separation of concerns.                                                                                                  â”‚

â”‚  # Account Management System Design for Trading Simulation Platform                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Introduction                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  This document outlines the design for a simple account management system for a trading simulation platform. The system supports account creation, deposits and          â”‚
â”‚  withdrawals of funds, transaction recording for buying and selling shares, and reporting of portfolio values and profit/loss.                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Required Modules                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  1. **UserAccount**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Responsible for managing user accounts, including fund deposits and withdrawals.                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  2. **Transaction**                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚     Manages the recording of transactions and enforces trading rules such as sufficient funds and share ownership.                                                       â”‚
â”‚  3. **Portfolio**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚     Handles the reporting of holdings, total value calculation, and profit/loss assessments.                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  4. **Market**                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚     Integrates with market functions, including fetching current share prices.                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## Module Details                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  ### 1. UserAccount Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `UserAccount`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `user_id`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      - `balance`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `create_account(user_id)` - Creates a new user account.                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      - `deposit(amount)` - Increases the balance of the user account.                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      - `withdraw(amount)` - Decreases the balance; ensures it does not go negative.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2. Transaction Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Transaction`                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `transactions`                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `buy_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the purchase of shares, checks if sufficient funds are present.                                                          â”‚
â”‚      - `sell_shares(symbol, quantity)` - Records the sale of shares, checks if the user owns a sufficient quantity.                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3. Portfolio Module                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  #### Classes and Functions:                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - `Portfolio`                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - **Attributes:**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      - `holdings`                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - **Methods:**                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `calculate_total_value()` - Totals the current value of all shares based on market prices.                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      - `report_holdings()` - Lists current holdings and their quantities.                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚      - `assess_profit_loss()` - Calculates and reports profit or loss from the initial deposit.                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4. Market Module                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  #### Functi...                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚  ### 2. Transaction Module                                                                                                                                               â”‚

    â””â”€â”€ ðŸ”§ Used Read a file's content (4)â•­â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ âœ… Agent Final Answer â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â•®
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Agent: Python Engineer                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Final Answer:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  ```python                                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  """                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  Trading Simulation Platform Modules                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Modules included:                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  1. UserAccount - Handles user account creation, deposits, and withdrawals.                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  2. Transaction - Manages buying and selling transactions.                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  3. Portfolio - Manages holdings and portfolio valuation.                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  4. Market - Fetches current share prices.                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Each module is self-contained and includes unit tests.                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  """                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  import unittest                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Market:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      """Market Module: Fetch current share prices."""                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      # Mock prices for demonstration. In real application, fetch from API.                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚      _prices = {                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          'AAPL': 150.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'GOOG': 2800.0,                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          'TSLA': 700.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'MSFT': 300.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'AMZN': 3300.0                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚      }                                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def get_share_price(symbol):                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          price = Market._prices.get(symbol)                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          if price is None:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError(f"Price for symbol '{symbol}' not found.")                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return price                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class UserAccount:                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚      """UserAccount Module: Manages user accounts and balances."""                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self, user_id):                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.user_id = user_id                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          self.balance = 0.0                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def deposit(self, amount):                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Deposit amount must be positive.")                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.balance += amount                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def withdraw(self, amount):                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Withdrawal amount must be positive.")                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          if amount > self.balance:                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient funds for withdrawal.")                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          self.balance -= amount                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Portfolio:                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      """Portfolio Module: Manages holdings and calculates portfolio value."""                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self):                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          # holdings = {symbol: quantity}                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          self.holdings = {}                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def add_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to add must be positive.")                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚          self.holdings[symbol] = self.holdings.get(symbol, 0) + quantity                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def remove_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to remove must be positive.")                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          current_qty = self.holdings.get(symbol, 0)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          if quantity > current_qty:                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError(f"Not enough shares to sell: {quantity} requested, {current_qty} available.")                                                              â”‚
â”‚          new_qty = current_qty - quantity                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          if new_qty == 0:                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚              del self.holdings[symbol]                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          else:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚              self.holdings[symbol] = new_qty                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def calculate_total_value(self):                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          total = 0.0                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          for symbol, qty in self.holdings.items():                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              price = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              total += price * qty                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          return total                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def report_holdings(self):                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          return dict(self.holdings)  # return a copy                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def assess_profit_loss(self, initial_deposit):                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          if initial_deposit < 0:                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Initial deposit cannot be negative.")                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          current_value = self.calculate_total_value()                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          return current_value - initial_deposit                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Transaction:                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚      """Transaction Module: Manages buying and selling shares with checking."""                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self, user_account, portfolio):                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.user_account = user_account                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio = portfolio                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          self.transactions = []  # list of dicts recording each transaction                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def buy_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to buy must be positive.")                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚          price_per_share = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          total_cost = price_per_share * quantity                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          if total_cost > self.user_account.balance:                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient funds to buy shares.")                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚          # Deduct funds                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          self.user_account.withdraw(total_cost)                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          # Add shares                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio.add_shares(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          # Record transaction                                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          self.transactions.append({                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              'type': 'buy',                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚              'symbol': symbol,                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚              'quantity': quantity,                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              'price_per_share': price_per_share,                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚              'total_cost': total_cost                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          })                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def sell_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to sell must be positive.")                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          # Check if user owns enough shares                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          current_qty = self.portfolio.holdings.get(symbol, 0)                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          if quantity > current_qty:                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient shares to sell.")                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          price_per_share = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          total_gain = price_per_share * quantity                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          # Remove shares                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio.remove_shares(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          # Add funds                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          self.user_account.deposit(total_gain)                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚          # Record transaction                                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          self.transactions.append({                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              'type': 'sell',                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚              'symbol': symbol,                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚              'quantity': quantity,                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              'price_per_share': price_per_share,                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚              'total_gain': total_gain                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          })                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  # Unit tests for all modules                                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚  class TestTradingSimulation(unittest.TestCase):                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def setUp(self):                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          self.user = UserAccount("user1")                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio = Portfolio()                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          self.transaction = Transaction(self.user, self.portfolio)                                                                                                       â”‚

â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ```python                                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  """                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  Trading Simulation Platform Modules                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Modules included:                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  1. UserAccount - Handles user account creation, deposits, and withdrawals.                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  2. Transaction - Manages buying and selling transactions.                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  3. Portfolio - Manages holdings and portfolio valuation.                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  4. Market - Fetches current share prices.                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Each module is self-contained and includes unit tests.                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  """                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  import unittest                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Market:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      """Market Module: Fetch current share prices."""                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      # Mock prices for demonstration. In real application, fetch from API.                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚      _prices = {                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          'AAPL': 150.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'GOOG': 2800.0,                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          'TSLA': 700.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'MSFT': 300.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'AMZN': 3300.0                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚      }                                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def get_share_price(symbol):                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          price = Market._prices.get(symbol)                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          if price is None:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError(f"Price for symbol '{symbol}' not found.")                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return price                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
