â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class UserAccount:                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self, username):                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚          self.username = username                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.balance = 0.0                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def deposit(self, amount):                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Deposit amount must be positive")                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          self.balance += amount                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def withdraw(self, amount):                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Withdrawal amount must be positive")                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          if amount > self.balance:                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient funds")                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          self.balance -= amount                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Market:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      _prices = {                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          'AAPL': 150.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'TSLA': 700.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'GOOG': 2800.0,                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          'MSFT': 300.0                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚      }                                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @classmethod                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      def get_share_price(cls, symbol):                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          if symbol not in cls._prices:                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Unknown stock symbol")                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          return cls._prices[symbol]                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Portfolio:                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self):                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          self.holdings = {}                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def add_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity must be positive")                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          self.holdings[symbol] = self.holdings.get(symbol, 0) + quantity                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def remove_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity must be positive")                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          if symbol not in self.holdings or self.holdings[symbol] < quantity:                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Not enough shares to remove")                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          self.holdings[symbol] -= quantity                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          if self.holdings[symbol] == 0:                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚              del self.holdings[symbol]                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def calculate_total_value(self):                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          total = 0.0                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          for symbol, qty in self.holdings.items():                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              price = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              total += price * qty                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          return total                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Transaction:                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self, user: UserAccount, portfolio: Portfolio):                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.user = user                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio = portfolio                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def buy(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity must be positive")                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          price = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          total_cost = price * quantity                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          if self.user.balance < total_cost:                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient funds")                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          self.user.withdraw(total_cost)                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio.add_shares(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def sell(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity must be positive")                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio.remove_shares(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          price = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          total_revenue = price * quantity                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          self.user.deposit(total_revenue)                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚          self.holdings = {}                                                                                                                                              â”‚

â”‚  without errors. The final content of the implemented modules is as follows:                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ```python                                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  """                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  Trading Simulation Platform Modules                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Modules included:                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  1. UserAccount - Handles user account creation, deposits, and withdrawals.                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  2. Transaction - Manages buying and selling transactions.                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  3. Portfolio - Manages holdings and portfolio valuation.                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  4. Market - Fetches current share prices.                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  Each module is self-contained and includes unit tests.                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  """                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  import unittest                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Market:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      """Market Module: Fetch current share prices."""                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      # Mock prices for demonstration. In real application, fetch from API.                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚      _prices = {                                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          'AAPL': 150.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'GOOG': 2800.0,                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          'TSLA': 700.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'MSFT': 300.0,                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          'AMZN': 3300.0                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚      }                                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def get_share_price(symbol):                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          price = Market._prices.get(symbol)                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          if price is None:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError(f"Price for symbol '{symbol}' not found.")                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return price                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class UserAccount:                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚      """UserAccount Module: Manages user accounts and balances."""                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self, user_id):                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.user_id = user_id                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          self.balance = 0.0                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def deposit(self, amount):                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Deposit amount must be positive.")                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.balance += amount                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def withdraw(self, amount):                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          if amount <= 0:                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Withdrawal amount must be positive.")                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          if amount > self.balance:                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient funds for withdrawal.")                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          self.balance -= amount                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Portfolio:                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      """Portfolio Module: Manages holdings and calculates portfolio value."""                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self):                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          # holdings = {symbol: quantity}                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          self.holdings = {}                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def add_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to add must be positive.")                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚          self.holdings[symbol] = self.holdings.get(symbol, 0) + quantity                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def remove_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to remove must be positive.")                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          current_qty = self.holdings.get(symbol, 0)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          if quantity > current_qty:                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError(f"Not enough shares to sell: {quantity} requested, {current_qty} available.")                                                              â”‚
â”‚          new_qty = current_qty - quantity                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          if new_qty == 0:                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚              del self.holdings[symbol]                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          else:                                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚              self.holdings[symbol] = new_qty                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def calculate_total_value(self):                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          total = 0.0                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          for symbol, qty in self.holdings.items():                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              price = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              total += price * qty                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          return total                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def report_holdings(self):                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          return dict(self.holdings)  # return a copy                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def assess_profit_loss(self, initial_deposit):                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          if initial_deposit < 0:                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Initial deposit cannot be negative.")                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          current_value = self.calculate_total_value()                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          return current_value - initial_deposit                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  class Transaction:                                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚      """Transaction Module: Manages buying and selling shares with checking."""                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def __init__(self, user_account, portfolio):                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          self.user_account = user_account                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio = portfolio                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          self.transactions = []  # list of dicts recording each transaction                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def buy_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to buy must be positive.")                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚          price_per_share = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          total_cost = price_per_share * quantity                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          if total_cost > self.user_account.balance:                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient funds to buy shares.")                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚          # Deduct funds                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          self.user_account.withdraw(total_cost)                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          # Add shares                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio.add_shares(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          # Record transaction                                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          self.transactions.append({                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              'type': 'buy',                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚              'symbol': symbol,                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚              'quantity': quantity,                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              'price_per_share': price_per_share,                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚              'total_cost': total_cost                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          })                                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      def sell_shares(self, symbol, quantity):                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          if quantity <= 0:                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Quantity to sell must be positive.")                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚          # Check if user owns enough shares                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          current_qty = self.portfolio.holdings.get(symbol, 0)                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          if quantity > current_qty:                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              raise ValueError("Insufficient shares to sell.")                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          price_per_share = Market.get_share_price(symbol)                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          total_gain = price_per_share * quantity                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          # Remove shares                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          self.portfolio.remove_shares(symbol, quantity)                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          # Add funds                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          self.user_account.deposit(total_gain)                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚          # Record transaction                                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          self.transactions.append({                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚              'type': 'sell',                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚              'symbol': symbol,                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚              'quantity': quantity,                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              'price_per_share': price_per_share,                                                                                                                         â”‚

â”‚  ### 1.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  This section allows users to manage their profile, security settings, and account preferences with ease and clarity.                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Profile Information Panel**                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Editable fields: Username, Email, Display Name                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    - Profile Picture upload option                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Security Settings Panel**                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Password change form (current password, new password, confirm new password)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Two-factor authentication toggle                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Account Preferences**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Notification Settings (email alerts, SMS alerts, etc.)                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚    - Theme selection (light/dark mode)                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - **Logout Button**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Use a sidebar or top navigation tabs labeled: Profile, Security, Preferences                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  - Content displayed in a clean form with clear labels, input fields, and action buttons                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  - Validation error messages displayed inline                                                                                                                            â”‚

â”‚    - Confirmation dialog before order is finalized                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Form and summary panel side-by-side on large screens, stacked vertically on smaller screens                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  - Highlight Buy and Sell buttons distinctly (e.g., green for Buy, red for Sell)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - Use tooltips or info icons to explain fields                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## General UI/UX Guidelines                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - Use a consistent color palette aligned with trading themes (e.g., green for gains, red for losses)                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - Ensure accessibility with keyboard navigation and screen reader support                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Responsive design to support desktop and tablet devices                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Loading indicators for data fetching sections                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - Error messages and success notifications clearly visible                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚  - User Account Management                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction History                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction Execution                                                                                                                                                 â”‚

â”‚  ## 1. User Account Management                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  This section allows users to manage their profile, security settings, and account preferences with ease and clarity.                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Profile Information Panel**                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Editable fields: Username, Email, Display Name                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    - Profile Picture upload option                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Security Settings Panel**                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Password change form (current password, new password, confirm new password)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Two-factor authentication toggle                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Account Preferences**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Notification Settings (email alerts, SMS alerts, etc.)                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚    - Theme selection (light/dark mode)                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - **Logout Button**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Use a sidebar or top navigation tabs labeled: Profile, Security, Preferences                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  - Content displayed in a clean form with clear labels, input fields, and action buttons                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  - Validation error messages displayed inline                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚  ## 2. Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Shows a summary of the userâ€™s assets, current valuations, and performance metrics.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Asset Summary Table**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Columns: Asset name, Quantity, Current price, Total value                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Sorting and filtering capabilities                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Performance Charts**                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    - Line or bar chart depicting portfolio value over time                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Pie chart showing asset allocation percentages                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - **Portfolio Metrics**                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Total portfolio value                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Daily change (value and percentage)                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Returns over selectable periods (1 day, 1 week, 1 month, etc.)                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Dashboard style layout with summary cards on top                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - Charts placed side-by-side or stacked depending on screen size                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  - Responsive design for desktop and tablets                                                                                                                             â”‚

â”‚  # Trading Simulation Platform UI Design Document                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  This document outlines the User Interface (UI) design for the Trading Simulation Platform focusing on the following functional areas:                                   â”‚
â”‚  - User Account Management                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction History                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction Execution                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 1. User Account Management                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  This section allows users to manage their profile, security settings, and account preferences with ease and clarity.                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Profile Information Panel**                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Editable fields: Username, Email, Display Name                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    - Profile Picture upload option                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Security Settings Panel**                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Password change form (current password, new password, confirm new password)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Two-factor authentication toggle                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Account Preferences**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Notification Settings (email alerts, SMS alerts, etc.)                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚    - Theme selection (light/dark mode)                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - **Logout Button**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Use a sidebar or top navigation tabs labeled: Profile, Security, Preferences                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  - Content displayed in a clean form with clear labels, input fields, and action buttons                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  - Validation error messages displayed inline                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 2. Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Shows a summary of the userâ€™s assets, current valuations, and performance metrics.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Asset Summary Table**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Columns: Asset name, Quantity, Current price, Total value                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Sorting and filtering capabilities                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Performance Charts**                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    - Line or bar chart depicting portfolio value over time                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Pie chart showing asset allocation percentages                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - **Portfolio Metrics**                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Total portfolio value                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Daily change (value and percentage)                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Returns over selectable periods (1 day, 1 week, 1 month, etc.)                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Dashboard style layout with summary cards on top                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - Charts placed side-by-side or stacked depending on screen size                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  - Responsive design for desktop and tablets                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 3. Transaction History                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Lists all past transactions with details and allows filtering and searching.                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Transactions Table**                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    - Columns: Date, Asset, Type (buy/sell), Quantity, Price, Total cost, Status                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚    - Pagination controls                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Search bar for filtering by asset or date range                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  - **Transaction Details Modal**                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Displays full details when a transaction row is clicked                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    - Includes related fees or notes if any                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Full-width table with fixed header and scrollable body                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  - Above table: filter controls including date picker and asset dropdown                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  - Clear visual status indicators (e.g., colors/icons for completed/pending/failed)                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 4. Transaction Execution Interface                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Enables users to buy and sell assets in an intuitive form.                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Asset Selector Dropdown**                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Searchable and categorized by asset types                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  - **Transaction Form**                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚    - Input fields: Quantity (numeric), Price (optional, defaults to market price)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - Buy and Sell buttons                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Order Summary Panel**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Displays estimated total cost including fees                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - Shows available balance                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - **Validation and Confirmation**                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    - Real-time validation of input                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    - Confirmation dialog before order is finalized                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Form and summary panel side-by-side on large screens, stacked vertically on smaller screens                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  - Highlight Buy and Sell buttons distinctly (e.g., green for Buy, red for Sell)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - Use tooltips or info icons to explain fields                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## General UI/UX Guidelines                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - Use a consistent color palette aligned with trading themes (e.g., green for gains, red for losses)                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - Ensure accessibility with keyboard navigation and screen reader support                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Responsive design to support desktop and tablet devices                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Loading indicators for data fetching sections                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - Error messages and success notifications clearly visible                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  This document should guide the frontend Python development to implement a user-friendly and efficient web application interface.                                        â”‚

â”‚  # Trading Simulation Platform UI Design Document                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  This document outlines the User Interface (UI) design for the Trading Simulation Platform focusing on the following functional areas:                                   â”‚
â”‚  - User Account Management                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction History                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction Execution                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
