â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 1. User Account Management                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  This section allows users to manage their profile, security settings, and account preferences with ease and clarity.                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Profile Information Panel**                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Editable fields: Username, Email, Display Name                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    - Profile Picture upload option                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Security Settings Panel**                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Password change form (current password, new password, confirm new password)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Two-factor authentication toggle                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Account Preferences**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Notification Settings (email alerts, SMS alerts, etc.)                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚    - Theme selection (light/dark mode)                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - **Logout Button**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Use a sidebar or top navigation tabs labeled: Profile, Security, Preferences                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  - Content displayed in a clean form with clear labels, input fields, and action buttons                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  - Validation error messages displayed inline                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 2. Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Shows a summary of the userâ€™s assets, current valuations, and performance metrics.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Asset Summary Table**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Columns: Asset name, Quantity, Current price, Total value                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Sorting and filtering capabilities                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Performance Charts**                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    - Line or bar chart depicting portfolio value over time                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Pie chart showing asset allocation percentages                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - **Portfolio Metrics**                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Total portfolio value                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Daily change (value and percentage)                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Returns over selectable periods (1 day, 1 week, 1 month, etc.)                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Dashboard style layout with summary cards on top                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - Charts placed side-by-side or stacked depending on screen size                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  - Responsive design for desktop and tablets                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚  ## 3. Transaction History                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Lists all past transactions with details and allows filtering and searching.                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Transactions Table**                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    - Columns: Date, Asset, Type (buy/sell), Quantity, Price, Total cost, Status                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚    - Pagination controls                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Search bar for filtering by asset or date range                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  - **Transaction Details Modal**                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Displays full details when a transaction row is clicked                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚    - Includes related fees or notes if any                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 3.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Full-width table with fixed header and scrollable body                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  - Above table: filter controls including date picker and asset dropdown                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  - Clear visual status indicators (e.g., colors/icons for completed/pending/failed)                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 4. Transaction Execution Interface                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Enables users to buy and sell assets in an intuitive form.                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Asset Selector Dropdown**                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Searchable and categorized by asset types                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  - **Transaction Form**                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚    - Input fields: Quantity (numeric), Price (optional, defaults to market price)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - Buy and Sell buttons                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚  - **Order Summary Panel**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Displays estimated total cost including fees                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚    - Shows available balance                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - **Validation and Confirmation**                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    - Real-time validation of input                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚    - Confirmation dialog before order is finalized                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 4.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Form and summary panel side-by-side on large screens, stacked vertically on smaller screens                                                                           â”‚
â”‚  - Highlight Buy and Sell buttons distinctly (e.g., green for Buy, red for Sell)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - Use tooltips or info icons to explain fields                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## General UI/UX Guidelines                                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  - Use a consistent color palette aligned with trading themes (e.g., green for gains, red for losses)                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - Ensure accessibility with keyboard navigation and screen reader support                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Responsive design to support desktop and tablet devices                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Loading indicators for data fetching sections                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚  - Error messages and success notifications clearly visible                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚

â”‚  # Trading Simulation Platform UI Design Document                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  This document outlines the User Interface (UI) design for the Trading Simulation Platform focusing on the following functional areas:                                   â”‚
â”‚  - User Account Management                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction History                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - Transaction Execution                                                                                                                                                 â”‚

â”‚  ## 1. User Account Management                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  This section allows users to manage their profile, security settings, and account preferences with ease and clarity.                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Profile Information Panel**                                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Editable fields: Username, Email, Display Name                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚    - Profile Picture upload option                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  - **Security Settings Panel**                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Password change form (current password, new password, confirm new password)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚    - Two-factor authentication toggle                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  - **Account Preferences**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Notification Settings (email alerts, SMS alerts, etc.)                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚    - Theme selection (light/dark mode)                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚  - **Logout Button**                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 1.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Use a sidebar or top navigation tabs labeled: Profile, Security, Preferences                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  - Content displayed in a clean form with clear labels, input fields, and action buttons                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚  - Validation error messages displayed inline                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ---                                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ## 2. Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.1 Overview                                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  Shows a summary of the userâ€™s assets, current valuations, and performance metrics.                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.2 Key Components                                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Asset Summary Table**                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Columns: Asset name, Quantity, Current price, Total value                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚    - Sorting and filtering capabilities                                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚  - **Performance Charts**                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚    - Line or bar chart depicting portfolio value over time                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Pie chart showing asset allocation percentages                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - **Portfolio Metrics**                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Total portfolio value                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚    - Daily change (value and percentage)                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚    - Returns over selectable periods (1 day, 1 week, 1 month, etc.)                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  ### 2.3 Layout Suggestions                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚  - Dashboard style layout with summary cards on top                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚  - Charts placed side-by-side or stacked depending on screen size                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚  - Responsive design for desktop and tablets                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚

â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def create_user(username: str, email: str, password: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          if username in Backend.users:                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "Username already exists."}                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          Backend.users[username] = {"email": email, "password": password}                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          Backend.portfolios[username] = {"cash": 10000.0, "stocks": {}}  # starting cash                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          Backend.transactions[username] = []                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          return {"success": True, "message": "User created successfully."}                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def update_user(username: str, email: str = None, password: str = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if username not in Backend.users:                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "User does not exist."}                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          if email:                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              Backend.users[username]["email"] = email                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          if password:                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚              Backend.users[username]["password"] = password                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          return {"success": True, "message": "User updated successfully."}                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def verify_user(username: str, password: str) -> bool:                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          return Backend.users.get(username, {}).get("password") == password                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def get_portfolio(username: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return Backend.portfolios.get(username, {"cash": 0, "stocks": {}})                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def get_transaction_history(username: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return Backend.transactions.get(username, [])                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def buy_shares(username: str, ticker: str, quantity: int, price: float) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if username not in Backend.portfolios:                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "User not found."}                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          portfolio = Backend.portfolios[username]                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          total_cost = price * quantity                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          if portfolio["cash"] < total_cost:                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "Insufficient cash balance."}                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          portfolio["cash"] -= total_cost                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          portfolio["stocks"][ticker] = portfolio["stocks"].get(ticker, 0) + quantity                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          Backend.transactions[username].append({"type": "buy", "ticker": ticker, "quantity": quantity, "price": price})                                                  â”‚
â”‚          return {"success": True, "message": "Shares bought successfully."}                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def sell_shares(username: str, ticker: str, quantity: int, price: float) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          if username not in Backend.portfolios:                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "User not found."}                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          portfolio = Backend.portfolios[username]                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          owned_quantity = portfolio["stocks"].get(ticker, 0)                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          if owned_quantity < quantity:                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "Not enough shares to sell."}                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          portfolio["stocks"][ticker] -= quantity                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          if portfolio["stocks"][ticker] == 0:                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚              del portfolio["stocks"][ticker]                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          total_gain = price * quantity                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          portfolio["cash"] += total_gain                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          Backend.transactions[username].append({"type": "sell", "ticker": ticker, "quantity": quantity, "price": price})                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return {"success": True, "message": "Shares sold successfully."}                                                                                                â”‚

â”‚          return "No user logged in."                                                                                                                                     â”‚

â”‚      return result["message"]                                                                                                                                            â”‚

â”‚  # Portfolio Overview                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  def get_portfolio_overview():                                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      username = current_user["username"]                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚      if username is None:                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          return "No user logged in.", "", ""                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚      portfolio = Backend.get_portfolio(username)                                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      cash_balance = portfolio["cash"]                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      stocks = portfolio["stocks"]                                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      stocks_str = "" if not stocks else "\n".join([f"{ticker}: {qty} shares" for ticker, qty in stocks.items()])                                                         â”‚
â”‚      return f"Cash Balance: ${cash_balance:.2f}", stocks_str, ""                                                                                                         â”‚

â”‚  # Transaction History                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  def get_transaction_history():                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      username = current_user["username"]                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚      if username is None:                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          return "No user logged in.", []                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚      transactions = Backend.get_transaction_history(username)                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚      if not transactions:                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          return "No transaction history available.", []                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚      history_list = []                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚      for t in transactions:                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          t_type = t["type"].capitalize()                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          history_list.append(f"{t_type}: {t['quantity']} shares of {t['ticker']} @ ${t['price']:.2f}")                                                                   â”‚
â”‚      return "Transaction History:", history_list                                                                                                                         â”‚

â”‚  # Transaction Execution                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  def execute_transaction(action, ticker, quantity, price):                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚      username = current_user["username"]                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚      if username is None:                                                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          return "No user logged in."                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      if quantity <= 0 or price <= 0:                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          return "Quantity and price must be positive numbers."                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      if action == "Buy":                                                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          result = Backend.buy_shares(username, ticker.upper(), quantity, price)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      elif action == "Sell":                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          result = Backend.sell_shares(username, ticker.upper(), quantity, price)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      else:                                                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          return "Invalid transaction action."                                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚      return result["message"]                                                                                                                                            â”‚

â”‚                      gr.Markdown("## Register")                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                      reg_username = gr.Textbox(label="Username", interactive=True)                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                      reg_email = gr.Textbox(label="Email", interactive=True)                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                      reg_password = gr.Textbox(label="Password", type="password", interactive=True)                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                      reg_password_confirm = gr.Textbox(label="Confirm Password", type="password", interactive=True)                                                      â”‚
â”‚                      reg_button = gr.Button("Register")                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚                      reg_output = gr.Textbox(label="Status", interactive=False)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                      reg_button.click(fn=register_user, inputs=[reg_username, reg_email, reg_password, reg_password_confirm], outputs=reg_output)                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                  with gr.Column():                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                      gr.Markdown("## Login")                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                      login_username = gr.Textbox(label="Username", interactive=True)                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                      login_password = gr.Textbox(label="Password", type="password", interactive=True)                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                      login_button = gr.Button("Login")                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                      login_output = gr.Textbox(label="Status", interactive=False)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                      login_button.click(fn=login_user, inputs=[login_username, login_password], outputs=login_output)                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚              with gr.Row():                                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                  gr.Markdown("## Update Profile")                                                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚                  upd_email = gr.Textbox(label="New Email (optional)", interactive=True)                                                                                  â”‚

â”‚                  upd_button = gr.Button("Update Profile")                                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚                  upd_output = gr.Textbox(label="Status", interactive=False)                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                  upd_button.click(fn=update_profile, inputs=[upd_email, upd_password, upd_password_confirm], outputs=upd_output)                                         â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          with gr.Tab("Portfolio Overview"):                                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚              cash_display = gr.Textbox(label="Cash Balance", interactive=False)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚              stocks_display = gr.Textbox(label="Stock Holdings", interactive=False, lines=5)                                                                             â”‚
â”‚              refresh_button = gr.Button("Refresh Portfolio")                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚              refresh_button.click(fn=get_portfolio_overview, inputs=None, outputs=[cash_display, stocks_display, gr.Textbox()])                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          with gr.Tab("Transaction History"):                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚              trans_header = gr.Textbox(label="History Status", interactive=False)                                                                                        â”‚

â”‚              history_button = gr.Button("Load History")                                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚              history_button.click(fn=get_transaction_history, inputs=None, outputs=[trans_header, trans_list])                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          with gr.Tab("Transaction Execution"):                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚              action_dropdown = gr.Dropdown(label="Action", choices=["Buy", "Sell"], value="Buy")                                                                         â”‚
â”‚              ticker_input = gr.Textbox(label="Ticker Symbol", interactive=True)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚              quantity_input = gr.Number(label="Quantity", precision=0)                                                                                                   â”‚

â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  import gradio as gr                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚  from typing import Dict, List, Any                                                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  # Simulated backend placeholders (to be replaced with actual backend integration)                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚  class Backend:                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      users = {}                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      portfolios = {}                                                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚      transactions = {}                                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def create_user(username: str, email: str, password: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          if username in Backend.users:                                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "Username already exists."}                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          Backend.users[username] = {"email": email, "password": password}                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          Backend.portfolios[username] = {"cash": 10000.0, "stocks": {}}  # starting cash                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          Backend.transactions[username] = []                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          return {"success": True, "message": "User created successfully."}                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def update_user(username: str, email: str = None, password: str = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                          â”‚
â”‚          if username not in Backend.users:                                                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚              return {"success": False, "message": "User does not exist."}                                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          if email:                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚              Backend.users[username]["email"] = email                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          if password:                                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚              Backend.users[username]["password"] = password                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          return {"success": True, "message": "User updated successfully."}                                                                                               â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def verify_user(username: str, password: str) -> bool:                                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚          return Backend.users.get(username, {}).get("password") == password                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def get_portfolio(username: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:                                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return Backend.portfolios.get(username, {"cash": 0, "stocks": {}})                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚      def get_transaction_history(username: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:                                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          return Backend.transactions.get(username, [])                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚      @staticmethod                                                                                                                                                       â”‚
